linguas="ar as be bg bn_IN bs ca ca@valencia cs da de el en_GB eo es eu fa fi fr gl gu he hi hu id it ja kn ko lt lv ml mr nb or pa pl pt pt_BR ro ru sk sl sr sr@latin sv ta te tg tr uk vi zh_CN zh_HK zh_TW ug "; \
for lang in $linguas; do \
  dir=/tmp/folks/pkg/folks/usr/share/locale/$lang/LC_MESSAGES; \
  /bin/sh /tmp/folks/src/folks-0.11.1/install-sh -d $dir; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo $dir/folks.mo; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo as $dir/folks.mo"; \
  else \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo $dir/folks.mo; \
    echo "installing ./$lang.gmo as" \
	 "$dir/folks.mo"; \
  fi; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo.m; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo.m $dir/folks.mo.m; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo.m as $dir/folks.mo.m"; \
  else \
    if test -r ./$lang.gmo.m ; then \
      /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo.m \
	$dir/folks.mo.m; \
      echo "installing ./$lang.gmo.m as" \
	   "$dir/folks.mo.m"; \
    else \
      true; \
    fi; \
  fi; \
done
